de l’issue de l’enfant qui vient dou large une main pendant	from the birth that occurs when a hand comes out during delivery.

se sens adonques que li tente l’ait perciet; et soit descoverte ou tu sens entre ton doit le syfac ou la char, adonques saiches qu’elle est persans;	Then you will sense that the tent has pierced it; and if you feel between your index finger the yolk or the heart, then you know it is vertical.
si n’i travillier mie c’on ne la puet saner.	If there's no confusion about which one it is, then you can't determine its nature.
On dist toutevoie c’on em puet bien saner aucuns, mais ce avient poc;	One can indeed properly heal most things, but this happens rarely.
et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit;	and the help that one provides, if it involves heating the delicate cautery according to the width of the fistula, as was explained previously;
et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu’il viegne delez le fondement; et faice ceu .ij. fois ou .iij., tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d’oiseil;	and hold the flame inside the fistula until it escapes from the base; and do this twice or three times, as long as you can tell that these burnt particles resemble a bird's feather;
et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char et soudant.	and then cleanse with wet cloths smeared in grease, until those burnt particles come out, then apply the ointment to bind and seal it.
S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien. Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez;	If he is healthy like this, it's good. If this, then otherwise cannot be healed;
et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur;	And if it is tested inside and doesn't pierce up to the root which is the foundation, and between your thumb and the tent you find a thick covering of flesh or fat, and when you see the fistula at that spot where there's no covering under the skin;
si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente;	If it covers from the beginning of the fistula and sticks right before the tent, then apply the cautery after that, until it reaches to the tip of the tent.
et sera delivré li tente, et cherra; puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.	And the tent will be freed and fall out; then remove those fat lumps that resemble a bird's feather, leaving none behind.
Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.	And if it doesn't affect you, and there is a cut between you and the wound, then apply either a fire cautery or a medicated ointment.
Car li cauteres de feu assemble .ij. bones choses: c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor;	For fire cauterizations consist of two main things: these include the brandishing of these heated rods, and bleeding the wound and drying out moisture;
puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe;	Then perform the treatment on wet cloths that have been dipped in grease or ground substances, as long as the limbs are bleeding, and let the heated rods burn inside them;
puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.	Then treat the wound with tourniquets made of thick leather, and apply dry medicines.
Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	For when it is restored, if it heals and does not return again.
Et se fistule vient jusc’a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu.	And if a fistula comes just up to the edge of the foundation, and is removed from the body, then cut at its base or foundation, and inquire about it.
Se tu sens la tente, et entre .ij. est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des .iii. manieres:	And if you feel the tent, and there is two of it or something similar, or it is about to pierce, but only has a way of faltering and hope left, through the administration of one of the three ways:
ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc’a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier;	or you cauterize it as we have said, or you cut until the bottom, or if you can use two tents and treatment in the first manner;
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit;	And do not go too far inward, that you might damage the structure holding the foundation, and allow the discharges to come through freely of their own accord;
puis le cure, si com nos avons dit;	then apply the cure, as we have said;
par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu’elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé;	By chance if it is clean, or you remove that covering and cleanse it then where it was removed from the foundation, either by trial or with another tool directed towards it;

puis estudie a restorer la plaie, et a demorer la fistule en la partie defuers le fondement: si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.	Then study to restore the wound, and to prolong the fistula in the lower part of the foundation: if it is lighter matter for the patient.
Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere: et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus,	And always make the tubercles in this manner: and when you press into the fistula and it is on or near the foundation beneath the skin above,
si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:	take a tent peg through the head according to this form:
Et i boute .i. fil tort en .ij., et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.	And I pierce two threads intertwined together, and push the tent peg along the entire length of the thread in the fistula until it reaches the head.
S’elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement;	If it's purely within the margin beneath the foundation inside, then extract the thread from that torn one, just as you bend your finger or foundation.
et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les .ij. chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse .i. jor ou .ij.;	and pull the head of the thread, and unite the two heads together, then hold one to the other, and let it rest for one or two days;
et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent;	and hold it in place each time until the threads have grown into those grooves that are between the two sides, and stick together.
puis cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit soudee et sanee.	then treat the wound until it is healed and clean.
Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.	If there is a fistula that does not pierce, make it pierce through all the ways you can, as long as it's not too deep.
Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	For there should be no need to make the insertion too deep beyond what is necessary, and then treat it, as we have said, until it heals properly.
Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d’une, part et trenchans;	The shape of the spinous spur from which the fistula is made is firm and small, and cutting into it;
et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:	And on another side, because there's no need to cut what shouldn't be cutted, as you see here:
des emorroydes	Of bleeding injuries
Emorrydes sont selonc ij. manieres: ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc,	Bleeding injuries can occur in two ways: either they are within the body's foundation, like a bit of resin, and there may be small or large ones, causing blood to flow out.
et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement; mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor,	Or if they are one or more, and extend beyond the body's foundation and to its head at that foundation; but those that extend so far have little moisture,
et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors;	Or they are accompanied by a bit of yellow water or a bit of blood, and have the color of purple;
et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il s’espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c’aperent li filz;	And the treatment for those who have them within the foundation, so you instruct the patient to let them grow until they reach chambers, as long as the foundations pass through them, and their filaments are visible.
si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines;	if you hurry, or you hold it with pincers, or you keep it by your nail, then remove it from its roots.
et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a .i. drapeil, ou a couton, ou d’une piece de chamelot;	and if the thorn cannot be held by its moisture alone, take it with two fingers, or with cotton, or from a piece of leather.
et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere;	and pull them out with your fingers, then remove them, and apply some warm powders that are used in cauterization.
ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, puis les cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	When you cauterize them as it is said or as per the chapter on cauterization, then treat with other treatments until they are clean.
et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu’il puist issir apertement;	And if the roots cannot come out, then cauterize the bladder cutting and grinding to wash what is or the roots, so that it may come out freely;
cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere;	If the bladder doesn't swell and if the threads are strong at the root, then the treatment is gentle;
et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez, et qu’il redoute l’incision par fer.	And you should take them with your nail or tweezers and pull them out, then treat them as we have said, until they are clean, and when there's fear of cutting by iron.
Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere: pren .i. fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l’aguille d’autre part, et torne les .ij. chiez dou fil desoz l’aguille,	If it is necessary that you stitch according to this method: take half a twist of thread and attach it to a needle, then guide the thread from above and pierce the needle from another side, and loop the two pieces of thread around the needle.
et si soit dou large; et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l’aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse .i. por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc;	and if you want it wider; and tighten the thread neatly, then tie the thread in a knot, and remove the needle, and do this for all of them, and leave one to drain off excess blood;
puis met sus le fondement .i. drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k’il repose;	then place on the wound one moist cloth in oil rose or plaster, and place it on the wound, and instruct the patient to rest;
et puis le laisse tant qu’il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d’oignement et d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And let it grow as long as it is scarce, and when they settle, if you treat with oil and other remedies, until it heals.
dou sechement dou fiens ou fondement	do drying through sweat or foundation
Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l’intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n’i vaut.	Many times, there is a drying in the intestines and due to the nature's compulsion, and when the disease is old and medication does not help.
Si covient que tu reses a la point d’un spatumile ou a ton ungle l’escorce desus, qui ne le laisse a moistir;	It is necessary that you clean up to the tip of a thorn or around your nail with the outer skin, which should not be left wet;
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sodez si com il covient;	Then the cure until it becomes firm as it should;
et s’il ne puet soder, si rencomence la rasure plus fort que devant, tant qu’il saine mout, et soit escorchiez;	and if it cannot become firm, then restart the shaving with more force than before, until some heal, and be burned;
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then continue the cure until it heals.
dou fremit	with shaking
Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;	Antennae are a small false appearance on the body, and they go forward;
et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.	And whenever it touches skin, one feels a sensation like death due to tremors, and it spreads throughout the body, and more in the hands than elsewhere.
Et li cure si est que tu pren une cainne d’une penne d’oie, ou une penne de vultul fort, et met celle caine sus le fremit, tant que li cercles porpreigne le fremit tot entor;	And the treatment involves taking a stick made of goose feather or a strong vulture's feather, and placing this stick on the tremors until the purple circle stops all the tremors;
puis torne ta main a tout la cainne tant que tu copes tout entor le fremit, et le met em parfont, et esraiche le fremit de ses racines.	Then twist your hand over the entire stick until you cover all around the tremors and place it forward, thereby eradicating the tremors from their roots.
Et se tu vues, si fai ceu d’une caine d’arain ou de fer selonc ceste forme, et soit subtilz desoz et traians desus:	And if you see it, do this to a spider's hair or iron according to this form, and let them be slender underneath and piercing above:
ne mie perciet, por mues tenir au doi, et mues presser Et se tu vues, si cauterize lou fremit, si com il est devant ou chapistre de cautere.	Don't pierce it, for you will hold onto both ends and squeeze it firmly. And if you see the twitching (of the wound), so like it is in front or chapter of the cautery.
de la forme dou clistere	in the shape of a bladder
Aucune fois fait on clistere d’argent ou d’archaut, ou d’arain fondut ou mailliet; et aucune fois fait on de ces estrumens petis et grans, selonc ces a cui il sont amenistrez.	Never make a bladder of silver or tin, or melted spider; and never make these small and large instruments according to their intended uses.
Cil donques c’on amenistre en la cure des enfans et qui sont foible et dolorous, sont petis.	Those then are treated in the care of children and those who are weak and painful, being small.
Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:	The form of the bladder is small on top and large below, or the belly is arranged in this way:
et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez; et ait a l’un des costez .ij. pertus, et en l’autre .i.;	and there is an opening where the belly might be squeezed, as you see, and the head might penetrate; and there are two small projections on one side, and one on the other.
et soit li ventres ou om met les medicines d’une vessie de beste ou de parchemin, et soit perciez tout entor de menus pertus,	and have the belly or place where we put medicine in a beast's bladder or parchment, and it should be pierced all through with small projections,
et ait entre chescun pertus .i. doit d’espaice, puis boute en ces pertus .i. fil fort de fil crut tort en .x. ou enqui entor, et assemble le ventre si com est une chievre;	And place between each piece one and a half inches of space, then insert in these pieces one thick thread made from woven linen for ten or fifteen times, and stitch the belly as if it were a goat.
et quant li medicine est dedens, si la lie a l’estrument devant d’un fil fort, puis clisterize; et c’est li forme dou cercle:	And when the medicine is inside, tie it to the tool with a strong thread first, then seal; and this forms like a circle:
Et soit li medicine ne trop chaude ne trop froide, et oint le chief dou clistere d’oile ou d’aubun d’uef, ou de semblant chose, puis le boute ens legierement;	And let the medicine neither be too hot nor too cold, and smear the opening of the curet with oil or yolk of egg butter, or something similar, then insert it gently;
puis l’espreigne li ministres a ses .ij. mains ensamble, tant qu’il soit toz vuis, puis estrai lou clistere, et lieve li malaides ses jambes a la paroit,	Then, with the doctor's two hands joined together, pull until you can see everything clearly, then remove the curet, and lift the patient's legs up to their chest.
et se li medicine vuet issir, si la teigne tant com il puet; et s’il dort une nuit atot, si est plus grans aide.	And if the medicine is to come out, it should be pushed as much as possible; and if he sleeps all night, that brings more aid.
Et se tu le clisterizes em maladie de decorrement de ventre, et li medicine se haste d’issir, si le rencomence tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if you have diarrhea due to a bowel obstruction disease, and the medicine hastens to come out, then repeat it until it is healed.
Et se li emorroide sont ou fondement, ou aposteme, si soit li clistere ausi subtilz com por .i. enfant;	And if there are hemorrhoids or a fistula, or an abscess, then use a catheter as thin as a child's finger;
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil sus coi li cuir soit estraint:	and it is the form of a thin catheter on which the skin is constrained:
des plaies	from injuries
Nos avons jai dit en la division la cure des plaies; or vos dirons les cures de mains et de medicine, selonc l’acomplissement.	We have discussed the treatment of wounds in the previous section; now we will discuss hand care and medicine according to their completion.
Je dis que les plaies sont diverses selonc ceu qu’elles sont faites, et selonc les leus ou les plaies sont faites, et de coi elles sont faites.	I state that wounds are various depending on how they were caused, and where they were inflicted, as well as the reason for their occurrence.
Les choses par coi plaies sont faites sont par gitement de piere, et taille d’espee et de couteil, ou de lance ou de fust ou de siette, ou de semblans choses;	The causes of wounds include impact from a stone, the strike of a sword or dagger, or by a spear, staff or cudgel, or similar things.
ou que sont faites selonc les leus dou cors, si com plaie que chiet sus le col, ou sus le chief, ou le peis, ou le ventre, ou le foie, et semblans membres;	The instructions are made according to the body's joints, for instance a wound that occurs on the neck, or head, or breast, or belly, or liver, and similar body parts.
et je vos dirai la cure de chescune plaie, et encomencerai as plaies dou chief simples, car li remenbrance venra en son chapistre.	And I will tell you the treatment for each wound, and begin with head wounds since memory will come to his chapter.
Je dis que quant simple plaie vient ou chief, et li os n’est brisiez, si pren garde se c’est de gitement de piere ou de semblans choses, et li cuir est toutevoie rompus et est li plaie grans,	I say that when a single wound comes or to the head, and if no bone is broken, be careful whether it's due to stone or similar things, and if the skin has been torn completely and the wound is large,
et tu doutes levement d’aposteme chaut: si le fai tantost sainier de la cephalique meismement s’il vient poc de sanc de la plaie, et soit li sainie au contraire de la partie navree;	and you slightly doubt about an abscess there: if it heals quickly after a scalp surgeon, even if there is little blood from the wound, and it gets healed in contrast to the necrotic part;
et eschuisse li malaides repletion de vin et de viandes grosses.	And the organs fill with wine and large meats.
Et s’il ne vuet sainier, si soit amenuisie sa viande, et ne boive point de vin, ne ne menjuce point de char;	And if it does not wish to improve, then reduce its meat intake, and do not drink wine, nor eat any flesh.
et met sor la plaie, se apostemes chaus i vient, coton moilliet en oile roset soulement, ou en vin stiptice;	And in the wound, if pus is present and comes out, use damp cotton soaked in rose oil or only in vinegar;
et s’il n’i a aposteme chaut, si met sus la plaie, s’elle est fresche a tout son sanc, et elle n’est muee par l’air, poudre, que je dirai un poc ci aprés;	And if there is no pus present and the wound is fresh with all its blood, and it's not being disturbed by the air, then apply powder, which I will describe a bit later;
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucuns oignemens, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the wound has healed, then apply certain ointments, until it is sound.
Et se li plaie est grans si com de tailleure d’espee et de semblans, et les levres ne se pueent assembler par tentes, si les assemble par cousture, si com je dirai as plaies dou ventre, de la costure.	And if the wound is large, like that of a tailor's cut and such, and the edges cannot be brought together with stitches, then join them by suture, as I would say about wounds in the belly, through suturing.
Se li plaie est descoverte de l’os, et pent, et ne tient mais que a un poc, si le cope; puis cure la plaie de medicine, et restoure char dure en leu de cuir,	If the wound exposes bone and muscle, and only holds together slightly when held in place, if it is closed. Then treat the wound with medicine, and replace hard flesh instead of skin.
et comande au malaide a mengier grosses viandes, si com testes et froment cuit, ausi com poulz, et semblans choses.	And instruct the patient to consume large meats, such as brains and cooked wheat, as well as chickens, and similar items.
Et se tu trueves ou cuir porriture, et il n’aert a l’os, si cope lou porrit tot, et giete fuer, puis le cure;	And if you find or leather corruption, and it does not reach to the bone, then cut out the whole corruption, and pour in some water, then clean it;
et se il ait artere en la plaie ou voine, dont sans cort, et il ne puet estainchier par medicines, si quier l’artere, et se tu la trueves desloie, si la lie d’un fil;	And if it have been an artery in the wound or vein, which cannot be stopped by medicine, then cut out the artery, and if you find that it is dislocated, tie it with a thread;
et se ceu ne profite mie, si la cauterize.	And if this does not benefit at all, then apply cautery.
Et se ces plaies sont petites et simples, si est li cure legiere: et est que tu mettes ens ceste poudre qui soude ainsois que li ars l’ait muee.	And if these wounds are small and simple, then the treatment is light: and you should put this powder on which bonds together like when the heat of it has spread.
Et li maniere de la poudre si est: pren encens une partie; sanc de dragon .ij. parties; chalz vive .iij. parties, et le poudre subtilment,	And here is how the powder is made: take some incense; dragon's blood .ii parts; powdered basil .iii parts, and finely ground it.
et emple la plaie, et l’estraint forment, tant qu’elle s’aerse bien et se joigne a tout son sanc;	And apply the powder to the wound, then press it firmly until the wound is well aerated and joins with all its blood.
et puis la lie bien, et la laisse sens desliier, s’elle n’enfle; car on n’oste la madicine tant qu’ele soit sanee.	And then cover it properly, leaving it to heal without any swelling; for the medicine is not removed until she is healed.
Et aucune fois fait on ceu de chalz soulement, quant on n’ait l’encens ne lou sanc de dragon, mais que li ars n’ait muee la plaie.	And this is done only once with charcoal alone, when one does not have the incense or the blood of a dragon, but that the surgeon has cleansed the wound.
Et se li ars ait mueit la plaie, meismement en esteit, si n’i met om mie ceste poudre;	And if the surgeon has cleansed the wound, even afterwards, one does not apply this powder at all;
mais met sus aucuns oignemens digestis, ou poulz de farine d’orge faites d’aigue et de miel, tant qu’ele giete bowe;	but instead applies some preparations as ointments, or oats flour made with water and honey, until it starts to heal;
puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	then continues other treatments until it heals completely.
Et se li brisure d’os vient avec la plaie, et elle est petite, si l’estrai as pinceures subtilz;	And if there is bone breakage with the wound, and it's small, then use fine needles to mend it.
et je vos dirai ci aprés les brisures dou chief.	and I will tell you about fractures of the head later.
de la plaie dou col	from the wound on the neck
Se plaie vient ou col et elle est simple, si n’a point de difference entre li et celi dou chief, mais se li ners dou col ou li artere est copee.	This wound comes from the neck and it is simple, if there is no difference between this and that on the head, but if the vein or artery in the neck is cut.
Se c’est li ners, si n’i a autre engien que laissier la cure, et n’i mettre nulle chose restraignant, car il nuit as ners et les fait retraire;	If it's the nose, if there is no other instrument than to let the cure alone, and not to put any restraining thing, because it harms the nose and makes it recede;
et ne mettre sus la plaie rien froit, car li substance des ners est froide, et li continuation d’aus si est avec le cerveil, qui est li plus haus membres;	And do not place anything cold on the wound, for the substance of noses is cold, and its extension to the head goes with the brain, which is the highest part of the body;
mais soit li medicine souez, si com chalz lavee en aigue douce, et mellee avec oile roset, et cucie lavee ausi en aigue douce,	but let it be warm medicine instead, such as charcoal washed in soft water and mixed with rose oil, and also wash the lettuce in the same soft water,
et autres pieres de mine selonc ceste maniere, et oignemens moistes.	And other stones of the mine according to this manner, and moist ointments.
Et se li plaie est grans, si la cout et lie de bendes, puis la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the wound is large, so that it needs to be bound tightly, then treat until it is clean.
Et se les plaies sont parfondes et ele est chevee et pleinne de bowe, si la perce ou plus bas leu;	And if the wounds are deep and full of pus, then pierce them or even deeper;
et se li artere est copee, et decorremens de sanc en vient, si la desoivre, et la loie, et la cauterize se mestier est;	And if the artery is cut and bleeding ensues, then open it and stop the bleeding; if necessary, perform cauterization as well;
et se li espinee de la gorge est copee, ou li keurs, et li conduiz est gardez, par coi la viande va,	And if it's cut from the throat or the knees, or if the guide is kept, by which the flesh goes,
si cout le keur sus la cainne de la gorge, et ne touchier la gorge mais la remet selonc sa figure naturel;	if you stitch the knee above the string of the throat, and do not touch the throat but set it according to its natural shape;
et puis l’estrain avenanment, et le laisse aucuns jors, puis le cure d’oignemens desechans tant qu’il soit sanez;	and then stitch the addition, and leave it for a few days, then treat with withering ointments until it heals properly;
et se li plaie a fait empression en l’os, si la quier;	and if the wound has formed in the bone, you should treat it;
et s’il i a pieces d’os, si les trai fuers toz se tu pues, et ces que tu ne pues avoir, si laisse tant que li plaie porrisse,	And if there are bone fragments, remove them thoroughly if you can, and leave those that you cannot retrieve until the wound heals.
et soit desevree et aligie li issue;	And evacuate it and strengthen its exit.
et se li plaie est fresche, si poudre sus la poudre que j’ai dit.	And if the wound is fresh, use the powder I've mentioned on it.
Et s’il a en la plaie os et il i a fistule, si la cure ensi com j’ai dit en son chapistre.	And if there's bone in the wound and there's a sinus, treat it as I have said in this chapter.
de la plaie de lance ou de coutel	from the wound of a spear or a knife
Se c’est cop de lance ou de coutel, et li plaie est parfonde, si regarde se de la plaie saut ventositez cant li malaides alainne: saiches adonques que li plaie est mortelz;	If it is a wound from a spear or a knife, and the wound goes deep inside, then look at the condition of the wound to determine if there's any wind escaping: knowing this means that the wound is mortal;
et s’elle n’est parfonde, et elle est fresche a tout son sanc, si n’i mettre mie a la premiere houre la poudre, ne ne la liier mie por le sanc que ne demorse em parfont,	And if it is not deep and its blood flows fully fresh, should one not apply the powder or bind it up in the first hour after, because the blood would not stop flowing from inside.
et reviegne au cuer, et ocie lou malaide;	and warm him to the heart, and rest the patient;
mais i met oignement atractif, et le lie .ij. fois le jor;	but I apply an attractive ointment, and fasten it twice a day;
et se tu n’as oignement, si met en la plaie viel coton por succier fuers la moistor,	and if you do not have an ointment, place old cotton in the wound to absorb moisture.
et fai dormir le malaide sus la plaie .iij. jors, ou .iiij., ou plusors;	have the patient rest on the wound for three days, or four, or longer;
si n’i venra mie spasme, ne tremor male de cuer n’es traingnemens d’alainne;	if no spasms, lack of heartbeat rhythm, or singular movements occur.
et quant tu vois les bones dispositions, si saiches que li plaie est sauve.	And when you see good conditions, know that the wound has been saved.
Cure la donques de tentes et d’autres cures, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Therefore treat it with various remedies and other treatments, until they are healed;
et s’elle ne puet saner, et oevre, adés saiches que il i a fistule; si la cure si com on doit.	and if it cannot heal and fester, then know that there is a fistula; treat it as one should.
Et se li plaie est d’incision d’espee ou de coutel, et elle est simple, ou pis ou au dos, si la cure de ceu qui est devant;	And if the wound is from an incision made by a sword or knife, and it is simple or worse, or on the back, treat it as the one in front would.
s’elle est grans, de cousture; et s’elle est petite, de poudre, et s’elle est empressee en l’os, et en a copeit pieces, si quier la plaie, et les trai fuers s’il sont desevrez;	If it's large, stitch it up; and if it's small, powder it; and if it's compressed in the bone, and has cut into fragments, clean the wound and remove any foreign bodies if they are present.
et s’il ne sont desevrez, si laisse porrir la plaie, si aligera li estractions;	And if they aren't removed, let the wound heal by itself, ease out the extrusions;
et des autres plaies as autres membres est li jugemens si com nos avons dit.	And for other wounds on other limbs, judge them as we have said.
dou derrompement dou ventre	Regarding the protrusion of the belly
Li derompemens dou ventre est grans et moiens et petis;	The belly's protrusions are large, medium-sized, and small;
de la grant plaie saut aucune fois li intestine, ou li ners des intestines, par coi li intromission d’aus;	From a major wound, it might cut the intestine, or its nerves, by which the organ invades;
et li costure est plus malaisie, et aucune fois vaut pis li petite plaie que li grans,	And the suture is more complicated, and nothing beats a smaller wound compared to a larger one,
por ceu c’on remet plus a poinnes les intestines en, s’on ne les i remet de chaut en chaut;	Because in this case, we don't put the intestines back into place as easily, unless they are returned gradually;
por ce que li intestine enflent tantost qu’il sentent le froit, si rentrent plus a poinnes,	Because when the intestines swell up just as they feel cold, they go back inside further.
et por ceu vaut mues li moieinne plaie, por ceu c’on ramoine mues l’intestine a son leu que as autres .ij.	And because of this, one must drain the infected wound, for if we move the intestines back to their place that the others do, it is good.
Et saiches que li routure dou ventre est selonc .iiij. manieres:	Know that the rupture of the belly occurs in four ways:
les .ij. costures communes avienent en la costure dou ventre,	The two common incisions occur at the abdominal seam,
et li costure des autres plaies dou cors et .ij. autres costures propres sont communes as autres plaies;	And the suturing of other wounds from the body, along with two other types of wound-specific suturings, are common for other wounds;
et toutevoie elles sont plus propres avec la costure dou ventre, et je dirai une chescune et declairerai.	And nonetheless, they are more precise when done on the abdomen, and I will describe each one and clarify them.
Je di que quant li plaie est petite, et aucune chose de l’intestine ist fuer,	I say that if the wound is small and there's nothing of the intestine exposed,
et griés chose est dou remettre, ceu est par l’une des .ij. manieres:	And when dealing with such injuries, this can be managed in one of two ways:
ou por la petitece de la plaie, si com nos avons dit,	because of the smallness of the wound, as we have said,
ou por ce que li intestine est enflez por le froit.	or because the intestines are swollen due to cold.
Et quant il est frois, eschaufez lou en teil maniere:	And when he is cold, warm him up in this manner:
moillie une esponge ou .i. mol drapeil en aigue tede soulement,	dampen a sponge or use one third of a cloth dipped only in water,
ou tu cuis en aigue squinant et cipre et spique,	When you cook with boiling water that splashes and contains myrrh and thorns,
et arose l’intestine tant que li enfleure soit ostee;	And let the intestine expand as long as the inner lining is perforated;
et aucune fois fait ce vins restraingnans, et est muedre que awe soule por desenfler.	And do not make this wine stop steaming, and when it becomes mature to relieve swelling.
Et quant tu vois l’enfleure departir, si amoiste l’intestine d’aigue ou altee et malves soient cuites,	And when you see the swelling depart, moisten the intestine with water that is hot or has been boiled and seasoned.
car par ceu est aligie li entree a poc de chose;	For with this there is very little room for error;
et s’il n’i puet entrer, si fent un poc la plaie a l’estrument de coi on cope les emorroydes;	and if it cannot enter, they make a slight incision with the tool used to remove the maggots;
et li premiere cure est muedre que li taille,	And the first treatment is to dry out the wound,
que nus n’i doit taillier sens grant necessiteit n’i ait;	that we should not cut it without great necessity, nor allow it;
et c’est li estrumens por le fendre:	And this is the instrument to split it:
si trenche dedens en la corbeure et defuer non, et vez ci la forme:	if you cut through the curve inwardly but not outwardly, and see this shape:
Et quant li plaie est enlargie, et li intestine saut fuer,	And when the wound is enlarged, and the intestines jump out,
si le remet arer selonc la forme naturel en son leu propre,	if you put it back according to its natural form within its proper place,
se tu en as pooir, car ce vaut mues.	then do so if you can, for this helps with movement.
Quant li plaie est large, et elle est en la partie desoz lou ventre,	When the wound is wide and it's on the belly area,
si covient que tu faices gesir lou malaide sus son dos,	if necessary, make the patient lie on their back.
et met ses jambes plus haut que son chief;	and raise his legs higher than his head;
et s’elle est en la partie desoz le ventre,	and if it's located on the abdominal area,
si met le chief et le pis plus haut que les parties desoz,	then raise the head and buttocks higher than the abdominal area.
et ausi se li routure dou ventre est en l’une des .ij. parties	and also if there is a rupture in the belly located in one of the two parts.
si met t’entente en ceu que li partie navree soit plus haute que li autre;	If you understand this, let the part that is removed be higher than the other;
et ensi covient amenistrer ceu que je dis en plaies grans et moienes.	And thus it should administer what I say in large and medium wounds.
Es plaies petites met ceu que t’est apparilliet,	Small wounds require this which is adapted to you,
puis aies entre tes mains .i. ministre pitous ki teigne toute la routure a sa main,	Then have in your hands a minister of plasters that heals the whole wound with his hand,
et assemble les levres;	And gather the lips;
et c’est la maniere commune de costures,	and this is the common way of stitches,
et est que tu preignes une aguille ou plusors, selonc la quantiteit de la largesce de la plaie,	and you should take one or more needles according to the width of the wound's quantity,
puis laisse des le chief de la plaie .i. doi d’espaice, et i fiche une aguille ou il ait .i. boin fil fort;	then leave at the start of the wound one inch in space, and I insert one needle with one good strong thread;
et perce les .ij. chiés dou cuir avec les .ij. chiés dou siphac,	And pierces both shoulder bones through the skin with both ends of the siphon wire,
qui est desoz le cuir dedens, tant que tu la faices percier de celle partie,	which goes through the skin from within, as long as you make it pierce that part.
et assemble les .ij. chief dou siphac les .iiij. ensamble;	and connect both ends of the siphon rod with three assemblies;
puis l’estrain d’un fil double entor l’aguille de .ij. pars,	then tighten a double thread around one needle for two parts,
puis assemble les .ij. chiés de la plaie avenanment,	then gather together both ends of the injury appendage,
et puis laisse .i. doi d’espaice, et i fiche une autre aguille;	and then leave one finger's width space, and insert another needle;
puis la lie dou fil si com tu as fait la premiere aguille,	then weave the thread in the same way you did with the first needle,
et ne cesser de ceu faire selonc ceu que tu as mestier des aguilles,	and continue doing this according to how you are skilled with needles,
tant que toute li plaie soit restrainte;	until all the wound is contained;
et soient les aguilles moienes, entre subtilz et grosses,	and are of needles that range from fine to thick,
car les aguilles subtilz copent toute la char, et les trop grosses si ne pueent mie bien entrer:	because the thin needles cut all the flesh well, and the too thick ones do not enter properly:
por ceu covient qu’elles soient moienes;	thus they should be of medium thickness;
et ne covient mie bouter les aguilles trop au defuer de la char et dou cuir,	And it is not proper to leave the needles too deep within the flesh and the skin.
k’elles ne copent et oevrent la plaie devant la soudure;	And they do not cut and spread the wound before the healing;
et puis cope les chiés des aguilles, qu’elles ne blecent lou malaide au dormir,	and then remove the heads of the needles, so they do not irritate the patient at night;
et i met tentes ou drapelz au chiés des aguilles por mues tenir,	and I place tents or cloths over the heads of the needles to keep them in place;
et les laisse tant que li plaie soit soudee;	And let them grow until the wound has healed;
et ceste maniere de costure as aguilles est plus covenauble en petites plaies,	and this kind of suture with needles is more suitable for small wounds,
car il i soffist une aguille ou .ij.	because it requires only one needle or two.
Li seconde costure si est commune,	The second type of stitching is common,
et est que tu assemble les .ij. chiés dou cuir et les .ij. chiés dou syfac ensamble a une aguille ou il ait .i. fort fil moien;	And it is that you assemble the two pieces of skin and the two ends of the flesh together onto one needle where there is a strong thread in the middle;
et quant tu avras perciez ces chiez toz .iiij. ensamble,	And when you have pierced all these pieces four times,
si ramoinne l’aguille a la partie ou tu as encomenciet, en la maniere c’on cout les dras;	then remove the needle from where you began, in the manner one sews with threads;
et met d’espaice entre chescune costure la grossece d’un menor doi;	and place a space between each stitch the size of one-third of a coin;
ceste costure sevent li home,	this stitch tightens the skin,
et je cousi une plaie c’uns hons avoit ou ventre,	and I sew a wound that had opened in someone's belly,
qui estoit navrez d’un coutel,	who was cut by a knife,
et estoit li plaie plus d’une palme de grant,	and the wound was larger than a palm in width,
et issoit des intestines bien .ij. palmes de grant,	and if they are of good length, two palms in fact,
et estoit li plaie enmi le ventre.	and it was located in the middle of the belly.
Je li ramenai l’intestine puis k’il ot esteit .xxiiij. houres fuer,	I returned the intestine to its place, and by that time, it had been twenty-four hours since it happened.
et fut li plaie soudee jusc’a .xv. jors, et le curai, et fut sanez.	and the wound healed up until fifteen days, and I treated it, and it became healthy.
Et li mire l’avoient jugiet qu’il morroit, et ce fut miracle;	And when the patient was thought to die, it became a wonder;
et ne le curai mie d’oignement, car je estoie en .i. leu ou on n’en trovoit point, ne nule medicines;	and did not cure it with ointment, for I was in one place where none could be found, nor any remedies;
et metoie sens plus sus la plaie coton viel .ij. fois le jor, et le lavoie d’aigue de miel tant qu’il fut sanez.	and changed the old cloth on the wound twice a day, and washed it in honey water until it healed.
Or vos dirai les .ij. propres manieres de cousture:	I will tell you the two proper methods of stitching:
pren l’aguille, et la boute des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens;	Take the needle, and start the thread from the outer part up to inside here;
quant elle a perciet le keur de droit en droit, si lai le chief dou siphac ou cousteit ou tu as bouteit l’aguille,	when it has pierced straight through to the bone, if it's at the siphon or costal area where you have inserted the needle,
et la fai percier d’autre part des la partie dedens jusc’a celi defuer;	and make it pierce from the inner part outwards to that external point;
et li entendemens de ceste costure si est que tu cous ausi com li peletier font les pelz,	and for this seam, do as the marten does with furs, by sewing it in such a way;
et que tu laisses une fois le syfac d’une part, et le reprent d’autre, tant que li costure soit toute acomplie.	And you must allow once the stitch on one side, and take it from another, until the suture is entirely completed.
Li seconde maniere de costure, que Galiens dist proprement,	The second method of sewing, as Galen correctly states,
si est si com aucun font, qui assemblent les .ij. parties ensamble naturelment,	If it is like what everyone does, who join the two parts naturally together,
et apploient l’un des chief dou syfac a l’autre chief, en teil maniere:	And they press one end of the thread to the other end, in this manner:
fiche une aguille ou chief dou mirach prochiene, et fai percier celui leu soulement,	Stab with a needle or pierce near Mirach's heart, and make sure to only pierce the left side.
et laisse les .ij. chiés dou syfac;	and leave the two shoulders free at the neck;
puis torne l’aguille, et la fai percier des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens,	then turn the needle and pierce it from below up to this depth inside.
as .ij. chiés dou syfac;	as the two shoulders at the neck;
puis fai percier l’un et l’autre des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens, en .ij. autres chiés dou mirach que sont on l’autre costeit;	Then pierce both from below at the outer part up to that inside, in two other shoulder joints which are opposite each other;
et c’est li muedre maniere de costure et li plus commune.	and this is the way it is sewn and the most common method.
Galiens si dist ceste parolle, et aucun le tesmoignent,	Galien says this word, and no one affirms it,
c’on doit coudre le ventre a .ij. aguilles, ou il ait fil en chescune;	One should stitch the belly with two needles, or where there is thread in each;
et doit on bouter l’une aguille d’une part, et l’autre d’autre, en la maniere de ces qui cousent corroies;	And it requires one to push a needle out from one side, and the other from the other side, in the manner of those who sew wounds.
et saiches que quant li routure est enmi lou ventre,	Know that when the rupture is within the belly,
si est li cousture plus griez que des autres leus dou ventre.	The stitches are more dangerous than those of other wounds in the belly.
Li jugemens de la plaie si est telz com li jugemens des autres plaies:	The judgment of the wound is as follows, just like the judgments of other wounds:
et est que quant tu trueves la plaie fresche a tout son sanc, ainsois que li ars l’ait muee,	And know that when you find the wound fresh with all its blood, as soon as the art has spread it,
si remet arer l’intestine, et lou cout; puis met sus la poudre enjanrant char,	if it is inside the intestine, and the cut; then put on the powder that makes it inflame,
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucun oignement que soit present, tant que li plaie bowe;	and if the art has spread it, apply no ointment until the wound heals over;
et chicent li fil, et soient soudez li sifac, et li mirach;	And stretch out the thread, and stitch up the skin, and bind with a bandage;
puis cure la plaie si com les autres, tant qu’il soit sanez;	then treat the wound as usual until it is clean;
et se tu n’as medicines, si met sus, tantost qu’ele comance a giter bowe, coton viel,	and if you don't have medicine, apply old cotton, as soon as it starts to ooze pus.
et le remue .ij. fois le jor tant k’il soit sanez.	and stir it twice a day until it is healed.
Car tu n’as mestier d’autre medicine en plusors dispositions cant les plaies sont simples;	For you need no other medicine besides when there are simple wounds;
et se tu doutes que li plaie ne faice communiteit as membres principelz,	and if you doubt that the wound will cause infection in major body parts,
si covient ke tu moilles lainne legiere en oile de tempree chalor, ou en oile roset,	then it is fitting for you to soak a light wool cloth in lukewarm oil, or in rose oil,
et la met entor les angres, et desoz les asselles;	and place it inside the armpits, and under the arse;
et s’il sent dolor ou porriture en bouelz, et maintes fois avient,	And if there is pain or rotting in the belly, and many times it happens.
si les clisterize de vin noir tede, et meismement se li porriture vient jusc’a l’intestine;	If black wine enemas are given, and similarly when such rot comes up to the intestine;
et le perce dedens, et saiches que quant c’est li gros intestines, si est plus legier a saner que li petis.	And if it penetrates deeply inside, know that when it's regarding the large intestine, it is easier to cure than the smaller ones.
Li intestine qui est apelez «jeun» ne puet saner quant il est navrez,	The intestine called "juvenile" cannot be cured once it is injured,
et c’est por la planteit des voinnes que i sont, et por la subtiliteit de tout le cors, et l’aprochement de sa nature des ners.	And it is due to the presence of veins that are present, and through the subtlety of all the body, and the approach of its nature to the nerves.
Et si li zirbe saut de la plaie, si le remet arrier ausi com l’intestine, tandis qu’il est fres;	And if the pus jumps out of the wound, then put it back behind in the same way as the intestines, while it is still fresh;
et s’il est vielz et devenus vers ou noir, si covient que tu lies le leu qui est noir, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne,	and if it has become old and turned red or black, then you should tie the part that is black, so that no bleeding comes thereafter,
car il i a voinnes et arteres;	because there are veins and arteries;
puis cope ceu qui est entre le liien,	Then take the one between the ligament,
et met les .ij. chiés pendans des la partie desoz la plaie jusque defuer por aligier l’estraction quant li zirbes chiet, et li plaie bowe.	and place both shoulders up to just beyond the wound area until they facilitate extraction when the ribs are pulled out, and when the wound is made.
de la routure dou boueil	from the rupture of the bladder
Quant li intestine est rons, et li plaie est petite,	When the intestines are intact, and the wound is small,
si la puet on restorer en aucuns homes,	if it can be restored in any houses,
por ceu que je vis que uns hons fut navrez ou ventre d’une lance;	for I see that some nobles were pierced or wounded by a spear;
et estoit li plaie au destre de l’estomac,	and the wound was on the right side of the stomach,
et fut envillie et devint fistule, et en issoit li egestion et li ventositez;	and it became inflamed and turned into a fistula, causing discharge and wind issues;
je i mis cure selonc ceu que je poi, et ne cessai de subtilier tant qu’il fut sanez, et li leus soudez.	I applied a cure according to what I knew, and didn't stop refining it until it was effective, and the patient was healed.
Et quant je le vis souder, je doutai que li malaides n’eust mal en son ventre;	And when I saw it healing, I wondered if the patient might have pain in their abdomen;
et il n’i ot point de mal, mais demora en millors dispositions, et menjans et bevans;	There was no harm, but it improved and ate and drank.
et dirent aucun experimentors que quant il a petite plaie en l’intestine, qu’il doit estre liiez en teil maniere:	And they would tell any experimenter that when there is a small wound in the intestine, it should be treated in this manner:
pren fremis a grans testes, puis assemble les levres de la plaie,	Take large thistles, then join the edges of the wound,
et quant li fremis ait overte la bouche, si la met sus les .ij. levres,	And when the thistle has opened its mouth, place it between the two edges,
si qu’elle estraigne sa bouche sus;	so that it closes its mouth upon;
et puis li cope la teste, et ce se tient si qu’il ne puet desliier,	and then cover its head, and this stays so that it cannot come loose.
puis met .i. autre fremit aprés en celle maniere que devant, tant que li plaie soit toute porprise;	Then after that shaking comes another one in this way as before, until the wound is fully taken care of;
et cout la plaie.	and till the wound.
Cil chief si s’aerdent en l’intestine, et ne vient nulle nuisance au malaide,	Those who are so hard in the intestine, and do not cause any harm to the patient,
et se puet on liier l’intestine d’un fil subtil qui est copez de l’intestine d’une beste,	And one can tie the intestine with a thin thread cut from the intestine of an animal,
en teil maniere:	in this manner:
pren le chief de cest fil d’intestine que soit mout descharnez,	Take the head of this thread of intestine that should be much shriveled,
et puis lie au chief de cest fil .i. fil de lin subtil tort,	and then tie to the head of this thread with a thin linen thread.
puis boute le fil en l’aguille, et en cout l’intestine, et le ramoinne en la routure;	Then thread the thread onto the needle, stitch the intestine, and set it during surgery;
et ceste maniere de costure de fremis nen est fuers que selonc la voie de fiance et d’esperance;	And this method of stitching wounds is done solely according to the path of faith and hope;
et se li plaie est grans et large, meismement quant elle est en l’un des grailes intestines, si n’i a engien ne santeit, fuer que subtiliteit.	And if the wound is large and broad, especially when it's in one of the intestines, if there is no obstruction or healing, ensure that it's due to the subtlety.
de fistule ou qu’ele soit	from a fistula, or if it is
Saiches que toute plaie ou aposteme, quant il enveillist, si est apelee universement «fistule»,	Know that every wound or abscess, as it matures, is universally called "fistula",
et meismement quant elle est chevee et rent bowe.	And similarly when it is sealed and begins to heal.
Et fistule est selonc la verteit nodation fautree dure et blainche, ou on ne sent dolor,	Fistula refers to a condition where there's a firm, hard, white swelling around the wound that doesn't cause pain,
et est ausi chevee com li penne d’un oiseil;	And it also grows like feathers from a bird;
et aucune fois en saut clere bowe, et autre fois espesse;	And no single time in a clear jump, and another time thick;
aucune fois poc, et autre fois assez;	Neither time faintly, and another time sufficiently;
et je en ai jai parleit en la division des plaies, que toute plaie que n’est sanee, et il n’i a char,	and I have spoken about the division of wounds, that every wound that is not healed, and there is no flesh,
ce n’est fuers que par une des .viiij. causes:	this is only due to one of the eight causes:
c’est a savoir, par la petitece dou sanc ou cors;	This means:
ou por sa malice;	or because of its wickedness;
ou por ceu qu’il i a char dure dedens, et sus les levres, que n’i laisse naistre char;	or because there is hard flesh inside and on the lips that prevents new growth.
ou il i a trop de bowe;	or because there is too much blood;
ou li leus est porris, et li matiere est de male qualiteit;	The ears are inflamed, and the substance is of poor quality;
ou li medicine n’est mie bone en la cure;	the treatment lacks good medicine;
ou por ceu que li corruption est maniere de pestilence;	or because the corruption takes on a manner of pestilence;
ou por la proprieteit en la region est tardive li digestion, et tarde li santeit, et enflee par nature;	or due to the property in the region being late for digestion, and delayed healing, and escaping naturally.
ou il i a voinnes ou os:	where there are veins or bones:

et se tu ne pues coper lou sein desoz si com tu vues,	and if you cannot cover the breast properly as you see,

si le cure de la cure de fistule, si com nos avons dit ci devant.	If the treatment for the pus-wound, as we have said before.
de l’aposteme de l’ungle	From the incision of the nail.

ou dou piet, ou par aventure naist en autres dois;	or on the foot, or accidentally forms in other parts;

Quant tu le cures si com nos avons dit en la division, et li cure ne profite mie,	When you treat it as we have instructed in the division, and the treatment does not benefit.

Li cauteres est mout grans aide se li os est sains, et li ungle est sainne;	The fire cautery is very effective if the bone is healthy, and the joint is healthy;
et se li ungle apresse la char ens, et l’encomence a poindre, et la blece,	and if the joint presses on the flesh and begins to pierce it, and irritates;

et se tu vois le doi corrumpre, si le cope en .i. des nous si com il est devant dit,	And if you see that the joint has rotted, then cut and remove it in one piece as we have discussed before,

la dolor dou sourdoit de la main	the pain deepens from the hand
Li dois ajostez qui naist en mains d’aucuns homes par aventure est toz charnus,	You must adjust what is born in the hands of some people by chance and are thick,
et par aventure i a teil ou il a osses, et aucune fois i a ungle,	and sometimes it has bone or lacks an angle,

Li soudemens que vient as dois ensamble vient par naissance, ou par soudement de plaie, ou par arsure de feu, ou par semblans choses.	The decisions that come together at the shoulder joint arise from birth, or due to injury, or through burning by fire, or through similar occurrences.

Des vils	Of low quality
Vis sont voinnes grosses envoloupees pleines de superfluitez melancoliouses, que vienent em plusors membres dou cors;	Vices are thick veins wrapped around the body filled with melancholic superfluities, that come from multiple members of the core;
et plus avient en jambes de ces qui vont a piet et qui travaillent et portent, que a autres.	And more occur in legs of those who walk and work and carry, than in others.
Il covient donques que tu li aministres aucune fois espurgement de cole, et puis le saine de la basilique.	It follows that you must administer one purging of bile to him, and then heal him with basilica.
Li cure de fer si est selonc .ij. manieres: l’une est c’on les cope, et traie on fuer le sanc noir;	The iron treatment has two methods: one involves cutting the wound and letting out black blood;
et li autre maniere si est que tu lieves la voinne, et la trai toute fuer.	And the other method is that you open the vein and let it bleed completely.
Li taille si est selonc ceste maniere: arose li premier la jambe d’aigue chaude mout fort, tant que li gros sans soit subtiliiez,	The bathing ritual proceeds as follows: immerse the first leg in hot water very strongly until the large veins become fine.
puis estrain la jambe dou malaide des desus la cuixe jusc’a la partie desoz le genoil;	Then hold the leg against the ailment from above the knee up to the part under the knee;
puis cope la voinne en .i. leu, ou en .ij. ou en .iij., d’une taille large,	Then cut the vein at one, two, or three units, depending on its width,
puis eslieve et trair fuer le sanc noir a ta main, des l’un chief jusc’a l’autre, tant que tant de sans en isse com li vertus dou malaide puet soffrir;	Then raise and drain the black blood to your hand from one end to the other, until as much blood comes out as the healing virtues of the ailment can bear;
et puis la lie, et li comande qu’il se teigne de viandes enjanrant cole noire;	And then place it (the wound), and instruct that it be oiled with black-cooked meat juices.
et recomence l’evacuation et la sainie quant les voinnes sont plainnes, et nuist au malaide.	And start evacuation and cleaning whenever the veins are filled up, and it harms the patient.
Li alevemens de li est selonc ceste maniere: reis la jambe dou malaide, s’il i a mout de poil,	The method of treatment is as follows: raise the leg from the patient, if there's hair;
puis le met ou bain, et li. arose la jambe d’aigue chaude tant qu’elle deviegne rouge, et enflent les voinnes;	Then immerse it in water, and raise the leg in hot water until it turns red, and the veins swell;
et se tu n’as point de baing, si le chaufe au feu, et puis le cope endroit la voinne dou lonc au chief dou genoil, ou en la partie desoz a la cheville;	And if you don't have water, heat it on the fire, and then apply the heated area along the length of the leg from thigh to ankle, or in the part below at the ankle;
puis aoevre le cuir a l’oncine, et escorche la voinne de chescune part, tant qu’ele apere quant on la sent;	Then cut the skin with a razor, and scrape the vein from each side, until you see it when you touch it;
et on la voit rouge et noire, et quant elle entre ou cuir si semble ausi com une corde blainche;	and you will see red and black, and when it enters the skin as well seems like a white thread;
puis boute le rait desoz, tant qu’ele soit alevee dou cuir, et puis la pent a l’oncine legier,	then cut with a knife until it rises above the skin, and then cut into it with a razor lightly.
puis le cope en .i. autre leu ensus iij. dois; puis escorche le cuir sus la voinne tant qu’ele apere,	then make another incision one-third above three inches; then scrape the skin over the vein until you can see it.
puis la lieve au rais, si com tu as fait, et la pent a un autre uncine, si com tu as fait premiers;	Then raise it on the rod as you did before, and proceed to another inch as you did at first.
puis cope une autre taille, ou plusors se tu en as mestier, puis la lieve, et la cope au doi dou piet,	Then take a different size or multiple if needed, then lift it and shape it on the thumb tip,
puis la trai et lieve jusc’a la seconde taille; puis l’estrai de taille en taille, tant qu’elle isse toute fuer, puis la cope;	Then guide and lift until you reach the second size; then gradually increase in size as much as it can withstand strength, then shape it.
et se tu ne la pues traire et lever, si i boute une aguille a tout .i. fil fort double,	And if you cannot guide and lift it, insert a needle at the end with two thick threads,
et la lie et la trai, et i boute desoz .i. rait, et torne ta main d’une part et d’autre, tant qu’il en isse;	And you will find it and pull it out, and push it off at a distance of one arm's length, and turn your hand from side to side until something comes out;
et garde qu’elle ne cope, car s’elle cope, si ne la puet on traire ne lever, et en vient nuisement au malaide;	And make sure it doesn't get stuck, because if it gets stuck, one cannot pull or lift it, and it causes harm to the patient;
et quant tu l’as toute traite, si met sor le leu de la plaie laine moillie en vin et en oile roset; et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when you have pulled it all out, place wet wool in wine and rose oil over the wound area; and treat it until it is clean.
Et se li vis est contraite et torte et envoloupee ensamble, et ele n’est mie droite, si com nos avons dit,	And if the limb is twisted and bent together as one, and it isn't straight, just like we have said,
si covient que tu la fendes tortement, mais ne la coper mie; et la trai si com nos avons devant dit.	If it is necessary for you to break it forcibly, but do not cover it; and treat it as we have said before.
Li forme dou fer dont on cope la vis si est corbes, et ne trenche mie, qu’il ne cope la voinne;	The shape of the iron with which you use the screw is bent, and does not cut, so as not to pierce the vein;
et est de grosse corbeure, car s’il estoit subtilz, si coperoit la voine, mais soit gros si com nos avons dit, et ci est li forme:	And it has a large curve, for if it were thin, it would pierce the vein, but make it thick as we have said, and this is its shape:
De la voinne civile	From the civil vein
Ceste voinne est enjanree en jambes, en chaudes parties ou il ne naist herbes ne arbre, et en terre ou il n’a point de moistor;	This vein is found in legs, in warm areas where no herbs or trees grow, and in soil without moisture.
et par aventure naist autre part qu’en jambes, et ceu avient de la porriture que vient desoz le cuir,	and may also arise elsewhere than on legs, and this happens due to the corruption that comes from below the skin,
si com il vient dedens le cors serpens et vers, enjanrez entre cuir et char.	likewise, if it originates within the body like snakes and worms, it manifests between the skin and flesh.
Et se li signes de l’encomencement de ceste voinne si est qu’il vient en la jambe une tres grans enflammation,	And if there are signs at the beginning of this vein's condition such as a severe inflammation in the leg,
puis se chainge li leus, et comence li voinne fors issir, ausi com une racine d’une plante.	Then change his limbs, and soon enough blood begins to flow out, like a root from a plant.
Quant li chiés apert, si covient que tu envoloupes entor une piece de plonc des une З et demi jusc’a .ij. З., et la noe,	When the shoulder is opened, it must be enveloped internally with a piece of plaster as long as half three and up to six inches, and then bind it,
et laisse le plonc pendant a la jambe, et totes les fois qu’il en ist point au defuer, si l’envoloupe entor le plonc, et la nowe;	let the plaster hang down on the leg and every time there is any shortage, cover it internally with plaster again and bind it.
et s’elle est trop longe, si en cope une partie, et envoloupe le remenant, et ne la coper mie en sa racine, tant qu’elle soit toute issue;	if it's too long, cut a part of it off and redo the plastering making sure not to cover its root until it's fully out.
car se tu la copes, si rentre en la char, et fait venir aposteme et porriture ou leu, et male maladie;	For if you handle it, it enters into the body, causing pus and decay or disease.
por la queil chose il covient qu’elle soit traite poc et poc jusc’a chief, et n’en remaigne rien ou cors;	By that thing, it is necessary to treat it carefully and cautiously until recovery, and leave nothing behind or injuries;
et est aucune fois ceste voinne quant elle est traite de .v. paumes de lonc, ou de .x.,	And there should never be a time when this vein is treated for as long as five palms, or for ten;
et uns hons vint ja a moi, a cui elle issit de .x. paumes de long, et quant tu la copes, si boute .i. rais ou pertus, et la perce jusc’a fons,	And I have experienced that when it is treated for ten palms, and when you handle it, if it lasts for one or more days after, and cuts it until the bottom,
si que tout en isse; et soit vuidie li matiere qui est dedens, et amenistre au leu medicines enjanrans porriture aucun jor, puis le cure si com les apostemes.	If everything proceeds as planned; and let the substance inside be drained, and apply remedies that combat putrefaction daily, then treat it like abscesses thereafter.
Et aucune fois a ceste voinne mains rains, et meismement quant elle apert en la jointure dou piet, ou ou piet,	And never use wet hands for this, and likewise when the leg opens at its joint with the foot, or the foot itself,
et i vient mout de pertus, et dont il saut rains; cure le donques si com nos avons dit devant.	And most of the injuries come from jumps and where they are wet; thus treat them as we have instructed before.
Des vers qui naissent entre cuir et char	Worms that emerge between skin and flesh
Ceste maladie est apelee en nostre terre «maladie de buef», por ceu qu’elle avient maintes fois as bués,	This disease is called in our land "beef illness", because it often affects cattle,
et est un petis vers qui naist entre cuir et char, et va par tout le cors montant et dessendant,	and a small worm is born between hide and flesh, and it travels throughout the body going up and down,
et le sent om bien a l’aler de membre en membre, tant qu’il desront le cuir ou il vait, et saut fuer;	and it is felt all over the body member by member, until it reaches the skin where it was going, and leaps out;
et est enjanrez de porriture d’aucunes humors, si com vienent vers et serpens et lumbris et ascarides ou ventre;	And it is infested with corruption from certain fluids, if snakes and worms and roundworms or maggots are entering the belly;
et doute on de son malice, car quant il va par le cors, et il monte au chief, et il vient a l’oil,	And there is doubt about his disease, for when it travels through the body, and ascends to the head, and reaches the eye;
par aventure rentre, et destruit l’oil; et ceu avient maintes fois.	By chance it enters, and destroys the eye; this happens often.
Quant tu le vues curer et traire, si ne puet on fuers que quant il vait:	When you see him being treated and drained, one can only wonder that when it was:
si covient donques que tu lies le leu desus et desoz d’un fort liien bien estroitement,	Therefore, it is necessary for you to bind it above and below with a strong bandage tightly.
puis cope sus et le trai fuer, et se li vers est em parfont en la char, et tu ne le trueves,	Then cut upwards and pull straight, and if it is properly inside the flesh, you won't find it.
si le cauterize de feu sus, tant qu’il muire;	If you apply the hot cautery to it, until it heals;
et li plus grans nuisemens que il fait, si est qu’il corront l’oil, si com nos avons dit;	And the most severe injuries that it causes, if they go into the eye, as we have said.
et se tu le vois venir ou chief pres de l’oil, si estraint desoz lui le sorcil forment, puis cope sus, et le trai fuer;	And if you see it coming or the head close to the eye, then restrain over him the eyelid, then lift upwards, and pull forcefully;
et covient user le malaide de mundifiement de cors de medicines solutives por les males humors porries,	And it is necessary to use the application of purifying oils from medicinal waters for the maladies caused by internal imbalances,
et se warse de viandes enjanrans porriture.	and if there are complaints about meats causing putrefaction.
De la dolor qui vient de ventositeit	Of the pain that comes from wind.
Ceste maladie est apelee en nostre terre «vakirir», et est une dolor que vient en aucuns membres,	This illness is called in our land "vakirir", and it is a pain that comes to any limbs,
et pues se mue de membre en membre; et je vis ceu que je vos di.	and spreads from member to member; and I have seen what I told you.
Je fui apelez a une femme malaide, et me descovrit som bras, et vis une petite enfleure en la voinne dou brais;	I was summoned to attend a sick woman, and she uncovered her arms for me, and I saw a small swelling in the arm vein;
et .i. poc aprés, li vis monter ausi com un ver a l’espaule,	and just an hour later, it rose as if by a worm to my shoulder,
plus tost que nulle chose, ausi com vif argent quant il cort de leu a autre;	Sooner than anything else, like quick silver when it is cut off from another;
li dolor se departit de celui leu, et se ficha en l’espaule,	The pain leaves that limb and penetrates into the shoulder,
et puis un poc aprés corrut par tout le cors, tant qu’ele vint en l’autre brais;	And then a little later spread throughout the body, until it reached the other arm;
puis me contait qu’elle tornioit adés entor le cors, si com je la vis.	Then I saw that it was spreading internally within the body as well.
Je me mervillai mout coment elle se movoit ensi de membre em membre, car je n’avoie onques veut ceste maladie selonc ceste maniere.	I was amazed at how she moved member by member in such a way, for I had never seen this illness done in this manner.
Toutevoie, je avoie veut maint que bien avoient veut movoir dolor de leu a autre,	In any case, I have wanted to establish many that well wanted to move the pain of their own to another's.
mais je ne l’avoie mie veut, si com je le vis en la femme;	but I did not want it like this, as I see in the woman;
et je me pensai que c’estoit por ceu que li femme avoit sec cors, et les voinnes descovertes,	and I thought that was because the woman had a soft body and her veins exposed,
et por ceu apparoit celle ventositez constrainte;	And because of this, a constraining wind appears;
et n’aperent mie selonc ceste raison a ces qui sont delicious, et qui ont moistes cors et voinnes reponues.	and do not appear according to this reason among those who are delicate, and have damp bodies and responsive veins.
Et quant tu vues curer ceste maladie, et li malaides sent celle dolor, s’elle t’apert si com nos avons dit,	And when you see the cure of this illness, and if the patient feels pain, if it appears to you like we said,
si la lie desus et desoz hastanment, et puis cope sus tant que cele ventositez constrainte au leu isse fuer;	if it increases upwards and downwards quickly, and then treat with remedies until that constraining wind leaves the body.
et cauterize le leu; et se tu ne la vois a tes eulz,	And apply a cautery to the wound; and if you cannot see it at your eyes,
si le cure de ceu qui deboute les ventositez, si com pilules fetides, et pilules de serapin, et semblans autres.	if one treats the dislocations of winds, such as stinking pills, pills made from rattlesnake venom, and similar others.
Des saiettes	From arrows
Les saiettes sont diverses, selonc lor semblances et selonc les leus dou cors ou elles chient.	The arrows are various, according to their appearance and according to the nature of the animal they come from.
Li diversitez de lor si est qu’il i a de celles qui ont grans pointes, et petites, et chevees, et soudees;	The variety of them is such that there are those with large tips, and small ones, some are hairy, and some are soldered;
et de celles qui ont .ij. angles, et de celz qui ont lengues, et de celles ou il a pieces;	and there are those with two angles, and among them are those that have tongues, and of those where there are pieces;
et celle qui chiet en aucun membre si chiet selonc .ij. manieres: ou en membre principeil cheveit,	and the one that defecates in no member does so according to two ways: or in the primary member it is hairy,
si com cerveil, cuer, foie, pormon, rains, intestine, vessie, et semblans membres.	just like the brain, heart, liver, lungs, kidneys, intestines, bladder, and similar organs.
Quant elle chiet donques en aucun leu de ces membres, et li signe de mort, que je te dirai ci aprés, t’aperent:	When she gives birth though, then not at any part of this body, and the sign of death, which I will tell you later, becomes apparent:
si covient que tu te warses de l’estraction de ceste saiette, car li mors vient aprés en plusors dispositions;	It is necessary that you prepare for the extraction of this arrow, because death comes after in various stages;
et quant cist mal signe ne t’aperent mie, et li saiette n’est mie em parfont, si la trai, et cure la plaie.	And when that bad sign does not appear and the arrow is not fully extracted, you should extract it and treat the wound.
Et li signe dou cerveil quant li saiette i chiet et perce l’os, et saut li syfac fuer qui est sus le cerveil,	The symptom of brain injury occurs when the arrow hits and pierces the bone, causing damage to the structure above the brain.
est quant scotomie et sode et esvertin et roujor ens eulz, et enflammation et roujor de lengue, et spasme et permixtion d’entendement, et vomissemens de cole;	When there is blindness and numbness and swelling in the eyes, as well as inflammation and redness of the tongue,
et per aventure ist sans fuer des narines, ou des oreilles; et par aventure pert la parole et la voix;	or perhaps affects the nose or ears; and by chance it deprives one of speech and voice;
et saut de la plaie moistor blanche semblant a poulz, et en saut ausi com bruee de char;	there is a white moist discharge resembling pus from the wound, and in this also like burned flesh from meat;
et se cist signe t’aperent, si te tien de la cure, et trai la saiette s’elle n’est ens.	and if you notice these signs, take care of the treatment, and pull out the arrow if it's there.
Li signe de la siette quant elle chiet ou cuer, sont qu’elle est pres de la mamele senestre, et sent ausi com s’elle estoit fichie en chose dure, ne mie vuide;	The sign of the arrow when it strikes or penetrates, is that it is near the left breast, and also feels as if it were stuck in something hard, not empty.
et par aventure li siette se muet ausi com li poulz, et en cort noir sanc, et vient froidor et suor froide, et sincope:	And by chance the arrow also stops moving like the hair, and causes black blood to come out, and coldness, and cold sweat, and fainting.
saiches adonc sens doute ke li mors dessent.	Therefore, with no doubt, know that the person is dying.
Et li signe de la saiette que nevre lou pormon est que sans plains d’escume saut de la plaie, et li gorge enfle, et li malaides mue color, et sospire haut et quiert le froit ar.	And the sign of the arrow that doesn't leave the body is that it bubbles up from the wound without much foam, and the throat swells, and the patient's face changes color, and they sigh loudly with their breath.
Et se li saiette chiet en la coverture dou pis, si est delez les petites costes; et giete grant alainne et grant dolor et sospire; et li muevent tuit li membre des espaules.	And if an arrow stops within the buttock's covering, it penetrates below the small ribs; and causes great pain and much agony, along with sighing; and all parts of the body from the shoulders move.
Et se li saiette chiet ou stomac, par aventure si saut de la plaie aucune chose de la viande indigeste.	And if an arrow stops in or near the stomach, by chance it may spill any undigested meat from the wound.
Et se li saiette chiet ou ventre, et en saut point de fien par l’intestine rout, si n’a point d’esperance en la cure, ne en l’estraction de la saiette.	And if an arrow stops in or near the belly, and it does not pass through the intestines on impact, there is no hope for treatment, nor in removing the arrow.
Et se li saiette chiet en la vessie, et li urine en saut et vient defuer, et li malaides sent fort dolor: saiches que li plaie est mortelz.	And if an arrow stops inside the bladder, and the urine flow is interrupted and spills out, causing great pain to the patient; know that this wound is fatal.
Li autre membre, si com li faice et li colz et li gorge et li espaule et li adjutoire et li espinee dou dos et li forcele et li cuixe et les jambes, et li membre semblant, sont sauf selonc plusors dispositions.	The other limbs, such as the arms and shoulders and neck and spine and ribs and hip and pelvis, and all similar limbs, are safe according to various positions.
Quant li saiette est en lou nerf ou l’artere, et elle n’est venimouse, si com je vos dirai qu’il m’avint, por ceu que vos faciez autretel.	When the arrow is in the nerve or artery, and it's not poisonous, as I will tell you what happened to me, because you did something else.
Il avint a .i. home c’une saiette li chut ou larmier en la racine dou neis:	It happened at two thirds of the distance that an arrow struck him in the armpit at the root of the nose:
je la tentai, et la traï d’autre part desoz la graisse de l’oreille, et fut sanez sens nusement.	I tested it, and tried to extract it from there across the fat behind the ear, and was left without any serious injury.
Et traï a un jeu une saiette que li chut en la graisse de l’oil desoz la papiere desoz,	And take an arrow to play with, let it fall into the oil grease underneath the paper over,
et li saiette estoit reponue, et n’en poi ataindre que la pointe devers lou fust,	And the arrow was returned, yet one could only touch its tip towards the shaft,
et estoit li saiette grans d’un arc turcois, a tout .i. fer legier sens oreilles; li jeus fut sanez, et ne li vint nulz mavais accidens.	And the arrow was large as a Turkish bow, weighing only one pound without feathers; the game was successful, and no ill events befell him.
Et traï une saiette de la gorge a un crestien, et estoit li saiette arabique a oreilles:	And take an arrow from the throat to a Christian, and this is the Arab's arrow with feathers:
je soiai les barbions, et subtiliai tant que je la traï, et fut sanez li crestiens.	I shaved them, and trimmed as much as I could during my treatment, until they were healthy for Christian people.
Et traï une saiette a .i. home, que li estoit cheue ou ventre, et pensai qu’il moroit;	And then extracted an arrow at one's body or stomach, and thought it was fatal;
et puis qu’il ot passez .xxx. jors, si ne mua point sa disposition;	and after it had passed thirty days, if it did not change its position;
je taillai sus la saiette, et l’engignai, et la traï fuer, et n’ot point de mavais accident.	I cut into the arrow, I set it in motion, and pulled it out, without any bad incident.
